What he presents instead is a **layered, mostly higher-order defensive structure built on a secure attachment substrate**, with one critical structural anomaly: his powers are wired to his autonomic state, which means that **when his defenses fail, they fail somatically and visibly to bystanders**. A breakdown is not interior. It electrocutes the person standing next to him, or it removes him from the visible spectrum. This fact has shaped, by selection pressure, every defense he has built since age thirteen.

What follows is an inventory ranked from most primitive (Vaillant Level 1 / psychotic-borderline) to most mature (Level 4 / adaptive), with frequency, behavioral signature, triggers, and observable tells. Each is rated as **POSITIVE** (functional, integrating) or **NEGATIVE** (cost-bearing, identity-eroding) or, most often, **MIXED**.

---

### 6.1 Primitive Defenses (Level 1) — *Largely Absent, Diagnostically Significant*

This is the first remarkable fact in the workup. The subject **does not deploy primitive defenses in any sustained way**. There is no splitting (he holds his uncle Aaron as both loving and predatory simultaneously, without collapsing the contradiction; he holds his father as both moral authority and contempt-issuer without flipping). There is no denial of reality (he *over-*acknowledges reality, particularly his own complicity). There is no psychotic projection. There is no acting out in the technical sense — his transgressions are exclusively *omissions* (secret-keeping), never *commissions*.

The single primitive defense that does appear is:

- **Somatic withdrawal via involuntary camouflage** (*USM* #3, #28; *Spider-Man* (2016) #6). Under acute panic he literally disappears. Phenomenologically this functions as a **psychotic-level defense expressed through biology rather than psyche** — the conversion of unbearable affect into literal invisibility. It is not chosen and it is not metabolized through fantasy; it is the body executing the wish *to not be here*. **RATING: NEGATIVE.** Tells: in the seconds before activation his breathing shortens, his shoulders draw inward, his weight shifts back onto his heels; the chameleon effect propagates from the torso outward, hands and face last. He has learned, by approximately age fifteen, to recognize the prodrome and to either lean into the camouflage tactically or to ground himself before it fires.

The corresponding aggressive primitive defense:

- **Venom-blast discharge under threat** (*USM* #4, #22, #28). The aggressive twin. Where camouflage = annihilation of self in the perceptual field, venom-blast = annihilation of the *other* in the perceptual field. He has electrocuted his uncle, friends, civilians attempting to comfort him. **RATING: NEGATIVE.** Tells: a brief stillness, fingers extending and stiffening, a small audible inhalation; the discharge is preceded by a half-second in which witnesses report the hair on their arms rising.

The two together constitute his **somatic primitive layer** — flight and fight rendered as visible biological events. Everything above this layer in the architecture is, in part, a system of higher defenses *built to keep this layer from firing*.

---

### 6.2 Immature Defenses (Level 2) — *Sparse and Atypical*

- **Idealization of Peter Parker.** The most clinically interesting defense in his file. He holds Peter (both the deceased Ultimate version, posthumously, and the 616 version, in person) as the standard against which his own legitimacy is measured. Peter has, on multiple occasions (*Spider-Men* I & II, *Spider-Geddon*), explicitly told him to stop. The idealization is **resistant to disconfirmation**, which is the diagnostic marker that it is doing defensive work rather than reflecting accurate assessment. **Function:** It externalizes the authority to be Spider-Man. As long as the standard lives outside him, he is not responsible for setting it, and his failures are failures-against-standard rather than failures-of-self. **RATING: MIXED.** Cost: retards his own authority development; produces deference that occasionally costs operational seconds. Benefit: gives him a stable ethical anchor in moments where his own judgment would oscillate.
- **Reaction formation against the "bad Miles."** Documented most clearly in the Ahmed run (*Miles Morales: Spider-Man* (2018) #10–25, clone arc). He is so preoccupied with the possibility that he is fundamentally his uncle's nephew that he over-corrects into conspicuous gentleness: pulls punches that did not need pulling, apologizes to combatants mid-fight, refuses tactical advantages that would feel "predatory." **RATING: MIXED.** Operationally costly; ethically generative. The Champions' organizing principle ("change without punching") is, in part, his reaction formation institutionalized.
- **Passive aggression.** Rare and weak, but present in his relationship with authority figures who have wronged him. He goes quiet rather than confrontational. Tony Stark in *Civil War II*: extended periods of unreturned communication rather than direct conflict. **RATING: NEGATIVE but minor.**
- **Somatization.** Sleep disturbance, appetite loss, headaches following major losses. He does not develop conversion symptoms in the classical sense, but the post-*USM* #200 period shows clear somatic discharge of grief. **RATING: NEGATIVE.** Tell: Ganke is the reliable detector — he notices the unfinished plates and the un-played games before Miles notices anything.

Notably **absent** at this level: projection (he over-owns rather than projects), fantasy-as-escape (he does not retreat into daydream — his fantasy life, where depicted, is mundane and reality-anchored), hypochondriasis, acting-out.

---

### 6.3 Neurotic Defenses (Level 3) — *His Dominant Operational Layer*

This is where the bulk of his defensive architecture lives. The neurotic defenses are the ones he uses *all day every day*, the ones that allow him to function under loads that would crater a less-defended subject.

#### 6.3.1 Compartmentalization / Secret-Keeping
The signature defense. He maintains, simultaneously, multiple non-communicating identity domains: Brooklyn-Visions-student-Miles, son-Miles, friend-of-Ganke-Miles, Spider-Man-Miles, nephew-of-the-man-who-died-fighting-him-Miles. The walls between these domains are managed with extraordinary precision — different vocabulary, different posture, different latencies of response. He is operationally bilingual across them. **RATING: MIXED, trending NEGATIVE over time.** It works until it doesn't; when domains breach (Rio recognizing him under the mask, Jefferson eventually learning), the cost is catastrophic. The defense was originally tactical, became a moral duty after Rio's dying instruction ("don't tell your father"), and persisted as a near-pathological structure even when its tactical and moral justifications had eroded. **Tells:** a half-beat pause before answering questions that cross domains; a tendency to answer the literal question and not the implied one; a specific micro-expression (gaze drops to the left, jaw sets) when refusing to elaborate.

#### 6.3.2 Intellectualization
Moderate. He thinks about his situation rather than feeling it, particularly in interior monologue. *Ultimate Comics* #200 and the post-Civil-War-II issues show extensive ratiocination about his own moral status that functions to keep the affect at arm's length. **RATING: MIXED.** Less developed than in Parker, who industrialized this defense. In Miles it is real but limited — he is not a natural intellectualizer and the affect tends to break through anyway.

#### 6.3.3 Rationalization
Present but weak. He is, notably, **bad at lying to himself**. When he rationalizes ("I'll tell Dad next week"), he knows he is rationalizing, and the knowledge corrodes the rationalization in roughly two-week half-life cycles. **RATING: low-impact NEGATIVE.** A more gifted self-deceiver would suffer less.

#### 6.3.4 Displacement
The *form* his anger takes when it cannot go where it belongs. Cannot be angry at his mother for dying, cannot be angry at his father for not knowing what to forgive, cannot be angry at Peter for dying and leaving him the bill. So the anger goes to: villains-of-the-week (with unusual intensity); to himself (chronic); occasionally to bureaucratic obstructions (school administration, SHIELD handlers). **RATING: MIXED.** It functions; it leaves the primary objects intact.

#### 6.3.5 Self-Deprecating Humor (Reflexive)
Distinct from Parker's outward-facing quip. Miles's humor is **primarily interior and primarily aimed at himself** — preemptive self-criticism that occupies the territory before others can. In dialogue it manifests as undercutting his own statements before completing them ("I mean — I don't know, that's probably stupid, but —"). In combat, where Parker quips at enemies, Miles is comparatively *quiet*; he tends to apologize to enemies (*Champions* #5, *Miles Morales* (2018) #3) rather than mock them. **RATING: MIXED.** Functional buffer; chronic erosion of self-presentation.

#### 6.3.6 Reaction Formation (Mature Variant)
At the neurotic level (distinct from the deeper reaction formation against being-his-uncle): he responds to his own urges to withdraw by *over*-engaging socially. Forces himself to text Ganke. Forces himself to sit with his family at dinner when he wants to be on a rooftop. **RATING: POSITIVE.** This is a healthy redirection.

#### 6.3.7 Undoing
Mild. After harsh thoughts about his father he performs small visible kindnesses (washes dishes, asks about Jefferson's day). After failing to save a civilian he over-engages with the next civilian. The pattern is recognizable to anyone tracking him longitudinally. **RATING: MIXED.**

#### 6.3.8 Isolation of Affect
He can describe his mother's death in flat operational terms when required (debriefs, conversations with Peter). The affect is genuinely walled off in those moments — not absent, but compartmentalized. **RATING: MIXED, with operational benefit and integrative cost.**

#### 6.3.9 Deference / Authority-Outsourcing
Borderline defense, classified here. He routes moral verdicts through external authorities (Peter, Cap, Jessica Drew, even an external prophecy — Ulysses's vision in *Civil War II*). This is not idealization per se; it is the broader pattern of treating others' assessments as more authoritative than his own. **RATING: NEGATIVE.** The most operationally significant of his neurotic defenses. The Civil War II arc is the keystone evidence: he treats a precognitive vision as *data about his own character* rather than as a single conditional probability about a future state.

---

### 6.4 Mature Defenses (Level 4) — *Well-Developed, Load-Bearing*

The presence and strength of this layer is what distinguishes him from peers and what allows the secure baseline to survive serial trauma.

#### 6.4.1 Sublimation
The mantle itself, properly understood, is sublimation. The guilt of inheritance, the fear of being-his-uncle, the survivor weight of Peter and Rio — all channeled into the construction of a hero identity oriented toward *saving* rather than *punishing*. **RATING: POSITIVE, foundational.** The Champions co-founding is the institutional form of this sublimation: he built a structure to protect other young heroes from the trajectory he is on.

#### 6.4.2 Altruism (True)
Distinguished from reparative over-helping (Level 3). At the mature level, his altruism is genuinely other-oriented: he derives stable, non-discharge-based satisfaction from civilian rescue, from mentoring younger figures in *Champions*, from his relationship with his cousin and family. **RATING: POSITIVE.** The tell: he does not need the saved person to know it was him. He does not photograph his own work the way Parker once did for the Bugle.

#### 6.4.3 Suppression (Adaptive)
He can set things down. Not bury them — *set them down*, return to them later. The Aaron material is suppressed, not repressed; he can access it in therapy-adjacent conversations (with Peter, with Ganke late at night, eventually with Jefferson). **RATING: POSITIVE.** Distinguishes him sharply from operators who deploy true repression.

#### 6.4.4 Humor (Mature Variant)
At the higher level his humor is genuinely affiliative — used to bond with civilians during rescues, to comfort younger heroes, to lower the temperature in Champions meetings. Distinguished from the self-deprecating reflexive humor of 6.3.5 by direction (outward, warm) and effect (connection, not deflection). **RATING: POSITIVE.**

#### 6.4.5 Anticipation
He thinks ahead about his own affect. He knows in advance that Mother's Day will be hard, that the anniversary of Aaron's death will be hard, that telling Jefferson the truth will be hard, and he prepares — clears his schedule, alerts Ganke, eats beforehand, plans the route home. **RATING: POSITIVE.** This is an advanced mature defense and unusual for his developmental stage.

#### 6.4.6 Affiliation
Under stress he *seeks people* rather than isolating. This is the single most important positive prognostic indicator in his file. Parker isolated; Stark drank; Banner ran; Rogers worked. Miles texts Ganke, calls Kamala, shows up at Peter's apartment. **RATING: POSITIVE, foundational.** The mature defense that the secure attachment baseline directly enables.

#### 6.4.7 Self-Observation
Increasingly developed across the canon. He watches himself, names what he is doing, and is capable (in measured moments) of correcting course. The Ahmed-run interior monologue is, structurally, a sustained self-observation exercise. **RATING: POSITIVE.**

---

### 6.5 Compensatory Mechanisms (Behavioral, Distinct from Psychological Defenses)

The defenses operate on affect and meaning. Compensatory mechanisms are the behavioral *structures* he has built around the defenses — the architecture of habit that supports the architecture of mind.

#### 6.5.1 Positive Compensations

- **The Ganke relationship as external regulator.** Ganke is, in effect, his depot of co-regulation. He functions as test-audience, reality-check, sleep-monitor, emotional ballast, and exclusion-zone (Ganke knows; the cost of secret-keeping is therefore lifted in one domain). The relationship is over-loaded but it works. **POSITIVE.**
- **Mentorship-seeking.** He systematically constructs a multi-source mentorship array: Peter (older brother, operational), Jessica Drew (peer authority on the Spider mantle), Cap (moral north), Kamala (peer co-thinker). This is sophisticated for his age and protects him against the failure mode of single-source dependency. **POSITIVE.**
- **The Champions as institutional self-permission.** Co-founding a peer team is, mechanically, a way to grant himself authority laterally rather than vertically — to be a leader-among-equals rather than to claim adult authority he does not feel he has earned. **POSITIVE, ingenious.**
- **Routinized family contact.** He maintains, even at operational cost, regular family dinners, regular check-ins with his mother, regular conversation with his father about non-superhero topics. The routine has the function of preserving the family domain as a real place, not a memory. **POSITIVE.**
- **Academic engagement.** He continues to take school seriously through arcs where most costumed peers would have let it lapse. The academic identity is a *legitimate non-borrowed* identity — one place he is unambiguously and ownership-fully himself. **POSITIVE.**
- **Eventual disclosure.** When secrets do come out (Jefferson, gradually; the family at large) he handles disclosure with care, takes the consequences, and the resulting reconfigurations *improve* his functioning. He has demonstrated capacity to dismantle his own most costly defense when conditions allow. **POSITIVE prognostic indicator.**

#### 6.5.2 Negative Compensations

- **Chronic over-functioning.** Patrols longer than necessary, takes calls he could decline, accepts responsibility for incidents he did not cause. The over-functioning is the behavioral form of guilt discharge. Sleep, schoolwork, and relationships all pay tax. **NEGATIVE.**
- **Help-asking inhibition.** He will not ask for help until catastrophe. Documentable across most arcs. The inhibition is fed by the belief that asking would expose his provisionality — that a *real* Spider-Man would handle it alone. **NEGATIVE.**
- **Acceptance of external moral verdicts as evidence.** The Civil War II pattern. He treats Ulysses's vision, Aaron's "you're just like me," Jessica Drew's early rejection, and even random civilian criticism as *data about his own nature* rather than as opinions to be weighed. This is the single most identity-corrosive negative compensation in his file. **NEGATIVE, primary.**
- **Romantic disclosure-failure pattern.** Relationships consistently end via secret-keeping pressure rather than relational dysfunction. He has not built a generalizable solution to the disclosure problem in romantic contexts. **NEGATIVE.**
- **Permission-seeking ritualism.** In team contexts he asks permission for actions he is entitled to take unilaterally. Slows operational tempo; trains teammates to treat him as junior longer than is warranted. **NEGATIVE.**
- **Pre-emptive smallness.** Physical posture under social stress: shoulders forward, hands in pockets or in front, weight slightly back, takes up less space than his frame warrants. The body is enacting the existential self-concept. **NEGATIVE, somatic.**
- **Abstention from disinhibitors.** Notable absence of any alcohol, cannabis, or stimulant use even in age-appropriate contexts. Reads superficially as virtue; analytically, it is **defensive abstinence** — he cannot afford disinhibition because his body fires weapons on emotion. The mechanism is protective but the cost is that he has never given himself permission to be loose, sloppy, or even fully adolescent. **MIXED, trending NEGATIVE for development.**

---

### 6.6 The Architecture in Operation: A Worked Example

Consider the disclosure-to-Jefferson sequence. Trigger: situation in which the secret has become operationally untenable. Sequence of defenses, in order of activation and failure:

1. *Compartmentalization* (6.3.1) attempts to hold. Fails because the domains have collided.
2. *Rationalization* (6.3.3) attempts ("not the right moment"). Fails on his own internal half-life.
3. *Displacement* (6.3.4) flares briefly — anger at peripheral targets. Self-noticed.
4. *Self-observation* (6.4.7) engages. He names what he is doing.
5. *Affiliation* (6.4.6) activates — he talks to Ganke first, then Peter.
6. *Anticipation* (6.4.5) — he plans the conversation, the location, the timing.
7. *Suppression* (6.4.3) holds the affect at workable level through the conversation itself.
8. During the conversation, *secret-keeping* (6.3.1) attempts last-minute reassertion; *self-observation* overrides.
9. After disclosure: *somatic discharge* — sleep disturbance, appetite loss (6.2 somatization), occasional involuntary camouflage flickers (6.1) in the following 48–72 hours.
10. *Altruism* (6.4.2) and *sublimation* (6.4.1) re-engage as he returns to the role with reconfigured ground.

The architecture, in short, is **front-loaded with neurotic defenses, well-buttressed with mature defenses, vulnerable to somatic breakthrough at the base**. The mature layer's strength is what makes him functional under his loads; the somatic vulnerability at the base is what would, in a worst-case future scenario, constitute the most likely failure mode.

---

### 6.7 Trajectory Assessment

Across the documented canon (2011–present), the defensive profile shows the following directional trends:

- **Primitive somatic defenses (6.1):** Decreasing frequency, increasing voluntary control. Camouflage and venom-blast are increasingly *deployed* rather than *suffered*.
- **Idealization of Peter (6.2):** Slowly attenuating but still active. Asymptotic decline rather than resolution.
- **Compartmentalization (6.3.1):** Decreasing across post-*Secret Wars* canon as disclosures accumulate. The cost of the defense has been increasingly recognized.
- **Self-deprecating humor (6.3.5):** Stable. Likely characterological now.
- **Authority-outsourcing (6.3.9):** The slowest-moving negative defense. Still substantially active.
- **Mature layer (6.4) overall:** Strengthening across the canon. The most encouraging trend in the file.

**Prognosis.** The defensive architecture is **age-appropriate-plus** — that is, more mature than developmental stage would predict, with a small number of clearly identifiable retardant patterns (authority-outsourcing, help-asking inhibition, pre-emptive smallness) that constitute the working edge of his unfinished business. The work that remains is **not the construction of defenses but the dismantling of compensations that were once protective and have become limiting**. He has the affiliative resources, the self-observational capacity, and the secure-base support to complete this work. Whether he does is a function of whether the operational tempo of his career allows the developmental room.

*End Section 6.*


## Longitudinal Psychological Profile

# UATU DOSSIER — SUBJECT: MORALES, MILES GONZALO
## Section 7: Longitudinal Psychological Profile

> *Methodological note.* The subject's published life is short in chronological years (debut age 13 in 2011; current operational age ~17 in main-continuity time, with reality-edit complications via *Secret Wars* 2015) but unusually dense in trauma-events per unit time. A standard "decade-by-decade" instrument is therefore reframed here as **developmental phase-by-phase**, calibrated to canonical issue arcs rather than calendar years. Each phase is examined across three orthogonal axes — *affect regulation*, *cognitive style*, *self-concept* — with the understanding that for this subject the three are coupled in a way that is somatically literal: his autonomic state generates measurable external phenomena (bio-electric discharge, optical camouflage). The psychometric instruments invoked (attachment classification per Main/Ainsworth; affect regulation per Gross's process model; self-concept per Markus & Nurius's possible-selves theory; bereavement per Shear's traumatic grief framework; impostor phenomenon per Clance) are real-world frameworks fitted to behavioral evidence in the canon.

---

### PHASE I — PRE-BITE BASELINE (chronological age 12–13; *Ultimate Comics: Spider-Man* #1, charter-school lottery sequence through pre-envenomation panels)

**Affect regulation.** Baseline is *unremarkable for a securely-attached pre-adolescent boy of high cognitive ability raised in an intact dual-earner household in Brooklyn*. Modulation strategies observable on-page are age-appropriate and primarily **antecedent-focused** in Gross's taxonomy: situation selection (he chooses to study, chooses Ganke as primary peer), situation modification (he negotiates Jefferson's permission to visit Aaron rather than going covertly — note that the *covert* visit comes later, and is itself a precipitating event). No evidence of pre-existing emotion-suppression: he cries when overwhelmed at the lottery announcement, hugs his parents without inhibition, expresses anger at his father's anti-Aaron stance directly rather than passive-aggressively. This is the cleanest affect-regulatory baseline you will find in a Spider-figure across either continuity, and it is the **psychological capital** he will spend down over the following four years.

**Cognitive style.** Verbally fast, lateral, ethically-tinged even pre-bite. Note the lottery scene: when his number is called he does not celebrate but immediately scans the crowd of children who did *not* win. The cognition is **other-referenced from baseline** — not a trauma-acquired hypervigilance to others' welfare but a *developmental given*, almost certainly internalized from Rio's nursing-profession modeling and Jefferson's redemption-narrative didactics. Intellectual curiosity is real but channeled (engineering interests, Lego-architecture with Ganke). No premorbid grandiosity, no premorbid rumination.

**Self-concept.** The bifurcation that will define him is already seeded: Aaron's frame ("you got lucky") and Jefferson's frame ("you earned it") are presented in the same issue, by the two men who structure his moral imagination. He has not yet chosen between them. The pre-bite self is therefore *un-adjudicated* — capable of being either a person whose goods are merited or whose goods are accidental. The bite is the event that forces the question, and he never settles it.

---

### PHASE II — ACUTE REFUSAL (age 13; *USM* #1–4, post-envenomation through Parker's death)

**Affect regulation.** Catastrophic decompensation, but in the form of **refusal** rather than dysregulation. He does not act out; he acts *not at all*. The defensive structure is **avoidance** in its purest form — situation selection escalated to situation *elimination*. He attempts to give the powers back (asks Ganke to help him find a cure). This is diagnostically rich: the first instinct of a securely-attached adolescent given god-tier abilities is to return them. Compare Parker's instinct (monetize → entertain → ignore). The difference is attachment-driven: Miles has a working family to protect, and his immediate threat-model centers on *exposure as freak*, not *opportunity*.

The somatic coupling first manifests here. Camouflage activates involuntarily under embarrassment in a school hallway — the body literally erases him when the mind wishes to disappear. Note that this is not yet labeled by him as a power; it is experienced as a **symptom**. The reframe from symptom to ability is months away. For now: his nervous system has acquired the capacity to externalize shame as invisibility, and shame is what he has.

**Cognitive style.** Constricted. Rumination loops emerge for the first time, organized around the question *what is wrong with me*. This is the **inaugural rumination set** and it is important because its content (defectiveness, wrongness, secrecy-need) will be the substrate onto which all later trauma-cognitions graft.

**Self-concept.** Catastrophically destabilized. The pre-bite "smart Brooklyn kid" frame cannot accommodate the new data. He has no script. Crucially, no aspirational frame is yet attached — he does not want to be a hero, does not fantasize about it, does not don a costume in private. The hero-self has to be *imported from outside* (Parker's death; the news coverage; the cultural availability of the Spider-Man role) because no internal hero-self pre-exists. This matters enormously for everything downstream: his Spider-identity is **exogenous** from the start.

---

### PHASE III — RELUCTANT ADOPTION & LEGITIMACY-SEEKING (age 13–14; *Ultimate Fallout* #4 through *USM* ~#20)

**Affect regulation.** A regulatory architecture begins to emerge under pressure. Because his powers fire on autonomic arousal, he is essentially **forced into early biofeedback training** — every panic attack risks discharging a stun-current into a bystander or vanishing mid-conversation. Within months of donning the costume he develops what would, in a clinical setting, be charted as **interoceptive awareness above age norms**: he can identify the somatic precursor to a venom-blast and abort it. This is the first instance of his trauma producing a *competence*. The pattern recurs.

Suppression (in Gross's sense — response-focused regulation) becomes overlearned. Smiling at his father while concealing the entire second half of his life. Hugging his mother after a near-death encounter on patrol with bruised ribs. The suppression is **selective and effortful**, not dissociative; he knows he is hiding, and the hiding has a cost he can name.

**Cognitive style.** Permission-architecture installs. The cognition *do I have the right* surfaces repeatedly — Jessica Drew's hostile interrogation, May Parker's eventual blessing, Gwen Stacy's acceptance. The fact that he *weeps* at the blessing is diagnostic: his legitimacy is conceived as something **granted by survivors**, not earned by deeds. This is **a self-concept architecture by adjudication** — others are the judges; he is the supplicant. It is functionally similar to what Beck would call externalized locus of self-evaluation.

Counterfactual cognition begins systematic operation here, and never stops. *If I had been there. If I had told someone sooner. If I were faster.* The counterfactual is the cognitive signature of survivor guilt; it will dominate his interior monologue for the rest of his published life.

**Self-concept.** Provisional, substitutional, derivative. He explicitly conceives himself as *standing in*. The Markus & Nurius "possible selves" framework is useful: most adolescents carry a constellation of hoped-for and feared possible selves competing for actualization. Miles carries instead a **possessed-by-the-dead self** — the hoped-for self is *Peter Parker, alive and operating* — and his own future-self imagery is conspicuously absent from interior monologue across this phase. He does not picture *himself* at 30. He pictures the role continuing.

---

### PHASE IV — THE AARON COLLAPSE (age 14; *USM* #22–28 and the year-plus retirement)

**Affect regulation.** Acute decompensation, then **shutdown**. The Aaron sequence produces, in rapid succession: (1) the discovery that a primary attachment figure has weaponized the bond; (2) a physical fight in which the attachment figure dies; (3) the dying transmission *you're just like me*; (4) his father, who does not know, expressing hatred for Spider-Man directly to him. This is a **maximally psychologically loaded** five-day window. His response is to take the suit off and put it in a drawer for a year-plus narrative time.

The withdrawal is not depression in the anhedonic sense — he goes to school, sees Ganke, functions — it is **role-amputation**. He has identified the Spider-self as the variable producing catastrophe, and excised it. This is, in fact, an *adaptive* short-term regulatory move; the problem is that the underlying guilt is not addressable through the amputation because the guilt is about who he *is*, not what he does. The role returns; the guilt was never about the role.

Affect during the retirement phase is **flattened but not absent**. He reads as muted on-page. Ganke's worry is the external thermometer.

**Cognitive style.** A new cognition installs and never fully decompresses: *people I love die in proximity to my mask*. This is technically a **post-traumatic cognition** in the Foa/Ehlers sense — overgeneralized, self-blaming, predictive of future harm. It does not meet PTSD threshold because it does not produce avoidance of broad classes of situations, only of the suit. But it is *the* organizing cognition for everything after.

Aaron's dying line is integrated as **evidentiary rather than manipulative**. A more grounded ego would file *you're just like me* under "dying abuser's last lie." Miles files it as data. This is the first hard evidence of the **outsourced moral verdict** pattern that Civil War II will later showcase. He cannot, structurally, dismiss external claims about his nature, because his internal verdict apparatus does not generate confident outputs.

**Self-concept.** Maximally destabilized. The pre-bite frames recur with new force: Aaron's "lucky" reframed as "lucky-and-corrupt-like-me," Jefferson's "earned" reframed as "earned by lying to your father." Neither parental frame survives the Aaron arc intact. He is left without a working self-narrative for the duration of the retirement.

---

### PHASE V — RETURN AND THE MOTHER'S DEATH (age 14–15; late *USM* through #200 / *Cataclysm*)

**Affect regulation.** The return to the suit is *not* a recovery; it is a recompression. He resumes operations with the Aaron cognition unmetabolized. Then Rio dies in his arms, recognizes him, and instructs him to keep the secret. This is the most psychologically consequential single panel-sequence in his canon.

The dying instruction does several things at once: (a) confirms that secret-keeping is *morally licensed by his mother*, retroactively sanctifying the lying as obedience; (b) installs a permanent association between *truth-telling* and *betrayal-of-the-dead*; (c) makes the secret a sacrament rather than a tactic. The downstream regulatory effect: secret-keeping is **no longer effortful**, because it is no longer questioned. The suppression load decreases because the moral question has been pre-answered.

This is a clinically dangerous development. Effortful suppression is metabolically costly but reversible; **moralized concealment** is cheaper to maintain but harder to unwind, because unwinding it requires defying not the self but the dead.

Acute grief somatics are textbook and well-documented in the post-#200 issues: sleep disturbance (depicted), reduced appetite (Ganke's commentary), social withdrawal calibrated to leave the friend-bond intact, intrusive recollection. By Shear's traumatic grief criteria he meets several but not all; the absence of suicidal ideation and the preservation of future-orientation keep him sub-threshold.

**Cognitive style.** Rumination intensifies, but a new mode appears: **bargaining-after-the-fact**. He runs counterfactuals not to plan but to torture. *If I had been faster, she would not have been there.* This is the bereaved person's loop and it persists long past the canonical resolution.

**Self-concept.** Brittle. The provisional self is now also a **culpable** self. Public Spider-Man competence holds; private self-evaluation craters. The bifurcation that will become his trademark — operational competence atop existential delegitimacy — fully consolidates here.

---

### PHASE VI — REALITY-EDIT INTEGRATION (age 15–16; post-*Secret Wars* 2015, 616 continuity, family restored)

**Affect regulation.** This is the most psychologically peculiar phase in the file. He retains the somatic memory of his mother's death; he occupies a reality in which she is alive. Canonically this is rarely addressed on-page, which is itself the diagnostic finding: he does not **process** the contradiction; he holds it. The regulatory strategy is **dissociation-in-the-mild-sense** (compartmentalization between two experienced realities), not pathological dissociation but a sustained low-grade splitting.

The observable behavioral residue: anxious overprotection of the restored family, hyperreactivity to threats against Rio specifically, a tendency to linger after embraces (depicted across multiple Ahmed-run issues), reluctance to leave family gatherings for patrol calls. He behaves around his mother as someone who is *checking she is still there*. Attachment behavior calibrated to a person who has already once vanished.

Affective ceiling rises slightly here — the family-intact baseline gives him more reserve than he had post-#200 — but the **floor** does not rise correspondingly. When he drops, he drops to the old depth, because the somatic memory is still there.

**Cognitive style.** A new cognition surfaces: *I am waiting for it to be taken away again*. This is the **future-oriented intrusion** characteristic of complex bereavement adapted to a survivor whose loss has been canonically un-done. The cognition is operationally identical to the standard "waiting for the other shoe to drop" of generalized anxiety, but its etiology is unique to him: he has empirical evidence that the shoe drops, because it has.

**Self-concept.** Slight consolidation. The 616-shift restores parental approval (Jefferson is no longer the man whose brother Miles killed in this continuity, at least not in the same way) and reduces one secret-keeping vector. He is *less* delegitimized, marginally, but the central structure — provisional, derivative, conditional — persists because it was wired in during Phases III–V.

---

### PHASE VII — CIVIL WAR II AND THE PROPHECY (age 15–16; *Civil War II* 2016)

**Affect regulation.** Brief but severe destabilization. Ulysses's vision of Miles standing over Captain America's body should, in a well-consolidated ego, produce *defiance* (this is not who I am) or *dismissal* (precognition is unreliable). Miles produces neither. He produces **interrogation** — going to Rogers, essentially asking *what should I do with this*. The regulatory failure is not affective (he does not melt down) but **epistemic**: he cannot generate the internal verdict that would let him dismiss the vision.

This is the cleanest exhibition of the **outsourced moral judgment** pattern in his file. The Aaron line ("you're just like me") was Phase IV's version; the Ulysses vision is Phase VII's. Both function the same way: external claim about Miles's nature → Miles treats as evidence → asks for adjudication from a higher authority. The pattern is so consistent it should be treated as a personality structure, not a situational response.

**Cognitive style.** Counterfactual cognition turns *prospective*. He has spent years asking *what if I had* — now he asks *what might I*. This is novel and worse. Retrospective counterfactuals torture but do not predict; prospective counterfactuals torture *and* paralyze.

**Self-concept.** The provisional self acquires a new feature: **potential-for-harm**. He has always feared being insufficient; he now also fears being dangerous. The two fears are not symmetrical and do not cancel — they compound. Operationally he is more cautious, more restraint-first, more de-escalating. This is part of what makes the Champions ethic land for him: it is a moral framework that **forecloses the prophesied outcome by design**.

---

### PHASE VIII — CHAMPIONS / GENERATIONAL CONSOLIDATION (age 16; 2016–2019)

**Affect regulation.** Substantial maturation. Co-founding the Champions with Kamala Khan and Sam Alexander produces, for the first time, a **peer regulatory environment** — affect-mirrors of his own age, with congruent ethics and similar guilt-loads. The presence of co-regulators (especially Kamala, whose ethical seriousness matches his) reduces the load on his own regulatory apparatus. He becomes visibly less brittle in team contexts than in solo ones. This is a real, measurable improvement.

He does not, however, claim leadership — he defers to Kamala. The deference is not cowardice; it is **role-comfort optimization**. He functions best as the conscience, the de-escalator, the friend-keeper. He resists every attempt to elevate him to formal authority across this phase. This is consistent with his core wound: authority requires the kind of self-trust he does not have.

**Cognitive style.** Begins to *articulate* his ethical framework rather than merely enact it. The Champions speeches, debate scenes, vote sequences show him doing something he did not previously do: **explicit moral reasoning aloud**. This is integrative work — the operationalizing of values that were previously held implicitly. It is one of the few unambiguously developmental gains in the file.

**Self-concept.** Marginal but real consolidation through **role coherence with peers**. He is one of several Spider-figures, one of several young heroes, one of several second-generation mantle-holders. The plural context normalizes the substitutional anxiety. He is *less alone in being derivative*, and this helps.

The idealization of Peter Parker, however, persists. Even in this phase, when offered authority by Peter directly (multiple *Spider-Men* sequences), he routes decisions through deference. Peter tells him, repeatedly and in varied phrasings, *you don't need my permission*. The cognition does not update.

---

### PHASE IX — THE CLONE ARC / SHADOW INTEGRATION (age 16–17; Ahmed run, 2018–2022)

**Affect regulation.** Tested at the limits. The introduction of Selim, Shift, and Mindspinner — fragments of him with his powers and (in the Selim case) his uncle's instincts — forces him into a regulatory scenario for which no prior phase has prepared him: he must remain emotionally regulated in the presence of *himself* behaving badly. The clones are walking provocations of his core fear (that he is Aaron-coded underneath).

What is striking is that he holds. There are decompensation moments — a venom-blast he later regrets, a panicked camouflage at a critical moment — but on the whole the regulatory apparatus built across Phases III–VIII does the work. He metabolizes the existence of the clones without breaking, and *chooses to take responsibility for them*. This is the closest thing in the file to a corrective emotional experience.

**Cognitive style.** First sustained engagement with **shadow material** in the Jungian sense. Where prior phases either avoided the bad-Miles possibility (Phase III–IV: don't be like Aaron) or dissociated it (Phase V–VI: I am the good son), this phase requires him to *look at it*. The cognitive style accordingly broadens: less either/or moral computation, more both/and. He begins to entertain the possibility that *bad capacities and good choices coexist* rather than the prior framework of *bad capacities must be perfected away*.

This is genuine cognitive development, and it is the first phase in which his thinking moves toward integration rather than purification.

**Self-concept.** The most important shift in the published record. By choosing to save the clones rather than disown them, he performs a self-recognition: *those are mine, including the bad parts*. It is not full integration — he still defers to Peter, still flinches at "real Spider-Man" rhetoric, still carries the Phase III provisional frame — but it is the *first* observable instance of him owning the dark material as **his own** rather than as **what he must not become**. The reaction-formation defense softens, slightly, for the first time.

---

### PHASE X — CURRENT BASELINE (age ~17; Ziglar run forward; disclosure-to-father metabolized; ongoing)

**Affect regulation.** The most stable he has been since Phase I, by a wide margin. The disclosure to Jefferson — when it lands, and lands well — removes the largest single suppression load he has carried since Phase II. Effortful concealment costs metabolic energy continuously; removing the largest concealment vector frees substantial regulatory bandwidth. He is observably less brittle, sleeps better (depicted), eats normally, laughs more readily.

The somatic coupling persists — anxiety still produces involuntary powers under high enough load — but the baseline arousal is lower, so the threshold is harder to cross. He has not had a Phase IV-magnitude decompensation in some time.

**Cognitive style.** The counterfactual loops are still present but **less commanding**. He can notice himself running them and abort. This is **metacognitive control above prior baseline** and it is hard-won. The Civil War II prospective-counterfactual cognition has largely receded; the Aaron retrospective counterfactual surfaces less.

He is, however, still measurably **other-referenced** in moral self-evaluation. The pattern that began in Phase III has not been extinguished, only attenuated. He still asks the older heroes. He still wants Peter's nod.

**Self-concept.** The bifurcation persists. The operational and existential self-concepts have moved closer together but have not merged. He is more willing, in present canon, to use the phrase *I am Spider-Man* in declarative rather than apologetic register. The frequency of *one of the Spider-Men* / *the other Spider-Man* self-locutions has decreased. These are small lexical markers of large internal shifts.

The central unresolved task — granting himself the permission to *be* Spider-Man rather than to *substitute for* one — remains unresolved. But the slope is positive, and has been since Phase IX.

---

### SYNTHESIS — THE LONGITUDINAL VECTOR

Plotted across the ten phases, three trends are clear:

**(1) Affect regulation: U-shaped then ascending.** Strong baseline (Phase I) → catastrophic stress-tests in Phases II–V → progressive rebuilding from Phase VI forward, with peer-context acceleration in Phase VIII and integrative gains in Phases IX–X. Current capacity exceeds pre-bite baseline in some respects (interoceptive awareness, metacognitive control of rumination) but remains vulnerable to specific provocations (family threat, "you're like X" framings, forced-choice scenarios).

**(2) Cognitive style: progressively more integrative, never fully consolidated.** From the constricted threat-monitoring of Phases II–IV through the explicit ethical articulation of Phase VIII to the shadow-engagement of Phase IX, the traj


## Psychiatric Assessment & Differential

# PSYCHIATRIC ASSESSMENT & DIFFERENTIAL — MORALES, MILES GONZALO

## Preamble: Framing and Methodological Note

The standard methodological hazard in evaluating costumed subjects is the *overdiagnosis trap*: the trauma load is so high that a careless examiner reaches reflexively for PTSD, MDD, or a personality disorder label, and the diagnostic noun then becomes the explanatory frame for the entire life. With this subject the trap is acute, because the trauma history is genuinely severe (predecessor's death at age 13; uncle killed in his presence by uncle's own weapon at ~13–14; mother dying in his arms with a final injunction to lie at ~14; serial near-death events; prophetic vision of himself as a political assassin at ~15) and the clinical picture is, despite all of that, *subthreshold across the board*.

The clinically accurate read — sustained over the canonical record from *Ultimate Comics: Spider-Man* #1 (2011) through the current Ziglar run — is that the subject is a **subclinically symptomatic but structurally well-organized adolescent**, in whom an unusually intact primary attachment system has buffered an unusually compressed serial-trauma exposure, producing trauma-shaped *features* without ever crossing into trauma-defined *disorder*. Diagnosing him as ill would obscure the actual finding: that he is, in psychiatric terms, a control case for what an adolescent with this exposure looks like when the developmental scaffolding holds.

The structure below proceeds: (1) what is present at sub-threshold or trait-level intensity; (2) what is conspicuously absent and the evidentiary basis for the exclusion; (3) the somatic/neurological complications unique to this subject; (4) longitudinal course; (5) the full differential against the conditions most likely to be incorrectly assigned; and (6) integrative formulation.

---

## 1. CONDITIONS PRESENT (Sub-Threshold or Trait-Level)

### 1.1 Prolonged Grief Disorder features (ICD-11 6B42 analog; DSM-5-TR Prolonged Grief Disorder)

**Status:** Features present, threshold not met by current criteria.

**Etiology and presentation.** Three death exposures structure the subject's grief load: Peter Parker (no personal relationship prior; grief is *vicarious* and *vocational*, driven by the conviction he should have been there — *Ultimate Fallout* #4); Aaron Davis (ambivalent attachment, killed in subject's presence by Aaron's own weapon malfunction during physical altercation Aaron initiated — *USM* #22–28); Rio Morales (primary attachment figure, died in subject's arms from collateral damage during the Cataclysm event, having identified him under the mask and instructed him to maintain the secret from his father — *USM* #200). The Rio loss is the only one that would, in isolation, support a Prolonged Grief diagnosis.

**Symptom profile post-Rio (*Cataclysm* through pre-*Secret Wars*).**
- Intense yearning, intrusive recollection cued by domestic objects.
- Identity-disturbance vignettes: subject ceases costumed activity for over a year, withdraws from Ganke, exhibits flat affect, struggles to occupy his own room.
- Difficulty re-engaging with previously meaningful activity (Spider-Man identity itself).
- Pronounced avoidance of trauma cues (specific locations in Brooklyn).
- Emotional numbness alternating with acute episodes.

**Why threshold is not currently met.** The post-*Secret Wars* reality-edit (*Secret Wars* #9, 2015) restored Rio alive. This is the rare clinical situation in which the *stressor itself was reversed*. The subject in 616 retains, however, somatic and procedural memory of the loss — implied across multiple Bendis-era and Ahmed-era beats in which he is depicted lingering at the kitchen door, watching Rio cook for an extra count, or freezing momentarily when she calls his name from another room. These are not Prolonged Grief criteria but they are *clinically continuous with* the post-loss period. The accurate framing is **resolved-by-ontological-rescue grief with residual hypervigilant-attachment features** — a presentation outside the diagnostic manuals, requiring sui generis description.

### 1.2 Survivor Guilt as Sustained Cognitive-Affective Pattern

**Status:** Trait-level, ego-syntonic, structural rather than episodic.

This is not a DSM diagnosis; it is a phenomenological finding with strong predictive validity for behavior. Documentable instances:
- Self-attribution of Parker's death ("I should have been there") despite no operational possibility of presence — *Ultimate Fallout* #4.
- Self-attribution of Aaron's death despite Aaron's documented aggression and weapon malfunction being the proximate cause — *USM* #28 and recurrently through the Bendis run.
- Self-attribution of Rio's death despite causation tracing to Galactus/Venom event variables wholly outside subject's control — *USM* #200ff.
- Anticipatory survivor guilt during Civil War II: the Ulysses vision is processed not as an external falsifiable claim but as evidence about his internal capacity for harm.

The pattern's stability across writers (Bendis, Ahmed, Ziglar) and across the universe transition argues for it being a *structural feature of the personality*, not an artifact of any single traumatic episode. It functions cognitively as a permanent low-grade tax on self-evaluation.

### 1.3 Acute Stress Reaction / Sub-Threshold PTSD Features (ICD-11 6B40; DSM-5 309.81)

**Status:** Acute features documented post each major loss; chronic features below threshold.

**Evidence per criterion cluster:**
- *Intrusion:* Documented post-Aaron and post-Rio. Nightmare imagery referenced; trauma-cued flashback in the alley scene where Aaron died.
- *Avoidance:* Significant — refusal to wear costume for >12 months post-Rio; avoidance of disclosure to Jefferson; route-changes around relevant Brooklyn geography.
- *Negative alterations in cognition/mood:* Survivor guilt (above); persistent negative self-evaluation ("I'm not really Spider-Man"); difficulty experiencing positive emotion ("waiting for the other shoe" — recurrent Ahmed-run interior monologue).
- *Hyperarousal:* Functionally indistinguishable from the operational vigilance demanded by the Spider-Man role. Cannot be cleanly attributed to trauma response vs. role demand.

**Why threshold is not met:** Functional impairment never reaches the criterion-required severity for sustained durations. He continues academic performance, maintains friendships, completes missions, retains future orientation. Symptoms attenuate over months (with help — Ganke, Peter, eventually Jefferson) rather than chronify. The integration trajectory is the wrong shape for PTSD proper.

### 1.4 Generalized Anxiety Features (ICD-11 6B00 analog)

**Status:** Trait-level, low-to-moderate, chronic, **other-directed**.

The worry content is diagnostic. Standard GAD presents with self-referent worry (health, finances, performance). This subject's worry is *almost exclusively* directed at harm coming to others: Ganke, parents, civilians, teammates, romantic partners. The dimension of worry is structurally identical to GAD but the object is consistently displaced outward.

Behavioral indicators: pre-mission checking rituals (depicted in Ahmed run — texting Ganke before patrol); reluctance to leave family events; somatic correlates (sleep latency mentioned by Ganke; appetite variability); inability to fully rest. The functional load is real but does not impair role performance — it *drives* role performance — and therefore does not meet GAD's impairment threshold.

### 1.5 Impostor Phenomenon

**Status:** Stable, robustly evidenced, non-clinical but behaviorally consequential.

Operational definition: the persistent internalized belief that one's competence is unearned and that one will eventually be exposed as a fraud, despite evidence of genuine competence. The subject meets this in textbook form, with the specific feature that his impostor anxiety has an *external referent* (Peter Parker) rather than being free-floating. The phenomenon's behavioral consequences are extensively documented:
- Deference to elder heroes past the point of utility.
- Permission-seeking from Parker, May, Gwen, Cap, Jessica Drew.
- Acceptance of the Champions' co-leadership rather than primary leadership.
- The "Kid Arachnid" rejection — he declines a diminutive but cannot fully claim the senior title either, settling on a name he treats as on loan.

Impostor phenomenon is *not* in DSM or ICD. It is included here because failing to name it leaves a major behavioral driver unaccounted for.

### 1.6 Somatic-Coupled Anxiety (Novel Clinical Entity)

**Status:** Subject-specific; no manual analog.

The bite produced a neurology in which the sympathetic nervous system is **electrically and optically externalized**: under acute fear or distress the subject involuntarily emits a bio-electric venom-blast or activates camouflage suppression. This is not "psychosomatic" in the usual sense; it is the literal coupling of an anxiety state to a discharge mechanism with environmental effects.

**Clinical implications, in order of importance:**
1. Standard anxiety presents internally and is observable only through proxy (sweat, tremor, speech). His presents *externally and consequentially* — people get hurt or he disappears. This creates a feedback loop in which anxiety produces consequences that produce more anxiety.
2. He has been forced to develop *adult-level* affect regulation by mid-adolescence as a public-safety requirement, not as personal growth. His emotional discipline is consequently overdeveloped relative to age but *brittle*: when it fails, it fails into one of two stereotyped modes (vanish or shock).
3. The two failure modes map cleanly to the avoidant/aggressive poles of fight-flight, with no available middle. He does not have access to a fawn or freeze response that is *invisible*; both of his available decompensation channels are visible to others and morally legible to himself.
4. He cannot use ordinary disinhibition strategies that other adolescents use to discharge stress — alcohol, intoxication, sexual acting-out, physical risk-taking-for-its-own-sake — because disinhibition is *operationally dangerous*. The absence of substance use in his file is therefore not abstinence-as-virtue but abstinence-as-necessity.

This finding has no DSM/ICD coding and must be carried forward as a free-standing axis of his picture.

---

## 2. CONDITIONS NOT PRESENT (Differential Exclusions)

### 2.1 Major Depressive Disorder — EXCLUDED

The post-Rio period invites a depression read and it is wrong. He exhibits **grief**, not anhedonic depression: he can still take pleasure in Ganke's company, still finds humor available, still maintains future-oriented behavior (school, friendships). His self-reproach is *event-specific* and *role-specific* (I failed her; I should not be Spider-Man), not the global self-condemnation of MDD. He is not psychomotorly retarded; he is *withdrawn*, which is behaviorally distinct. There is no documented suicidal ideation across the canon — a notable absence given the load. Sleep and appetite disturbances are present but proportionate to bereavement and remit. The episodes are reactive and bounded; they lack the autonomous, free-running character of a Major Depressive Episode.

### 2.2 PTSD Proper — EXCLUDED

He has every ingredient: Criterion A stressors in multiples; intrusion symptoms; avoidance; negative cognitions; hyperarousal. He does not have **the disorder**, because:
- The cluster fails to persist beyond one month at full criterion severity.
- He demonstrates **integration**, not dissociation. Trauma material is consciously available, narratable, and used in subsequent decision-making. He does not exhibit derealization, depersonalization, or amnestic gaps.
- Functional impairment is short of criterion threshold; role performance is preserved or enhanced.
- The trauma is metabolized into identity (often pathologically — see survivor guilt) rather than walled off from identity.

This is the most important exclusion because PTSD is the diagnosis casual readers reach for first, and it is wrong. He has trauma; he is not a PTSD case.

### 2.3 Cluster B Personality Pathology — EXCLUDED ACROSS ALL FOUR

**Antisocial PD:** Excluded on every criterion. No deceitfulness for personal gain (secret-keeping is protective, not exploitative). No impulsivity. No aggressiveness (the opposite — chronic de-escalation). No reckless disregard for others' safety (chronic *excess* concern). No irresponsibility. No lack of remorse (excess remorse). The "you're just like me" line is canon's diagnostic red herring; it should be read as *Aaron's* projective identification, not as evidence.

**Borderline PD:** Excluded. His identity disturbance is *underclaimed*, not unstable. BPD identity disturbance presents as oscillating, contradictory, mood-driven self-states; his presents as a *single stable self-concept* he believes is insufficient. He does not exhibit splitting (he holds ambivalent views of Aaron and even of himself in integrated form), abandonment terror (he tolerates Peter's absences, separations from family), impulsive self-damaging behavior, or affective instability of the BPD type. His emotional life is over-regulated, not under-regulated.

**Narcissistic PD:** Excluded with prejudice. The picture is the photographic negative: grandiosity → impostor anxiety; entitlement → permission-seeking; exploitative interpersonal style → reparative interpersonal style; lack of empathy → empathic hypertrophy.

**Histrionic PD:** Not applicable. No attention-seeking, no sexualized self-presentation, no shallow affect.

### 2.4 Cluster A Personality Pathology — EXCLUDED

No paranoid features (he trusts almost too easily). No schizoid features (deep relational engagement). No schizotypal features (no magical thinking outside the operationally appropriate; no perceptual oddities; speech and affect within normative range).

### 2.5 Cluster C Personality Pathology — PARTIAL TRAIT, NOT DISORDER

There are mildly **dependent** features (deference to elder heroes, permission-seeking) and mildly **obsessive-compulsive personality** features (over-conscientiousness, moral rigidity around the no-kill rule). Neither approaches diagnostic threshold. The dependent features are role-and-age appropriate; the OCPD-like features are values-driven and ego-syntonic in a way that distinguishes them from clinical OCPD.

### 2.6 OCD — EXCLUDED

The secret-keeping behavior could be mistaken for compulsive ritual. It is not. Obsessive-compulsive compulsions are ego-dystonic, anxiety-driven, and disconnected from rational justification. His secret-keeping is **ego-syntonic, value-driven, and rationally instrumented** within his frame (he believes disclosure will harm specific named persons in specific ways). His pre-mission checking behaviors are tactical, not ritualistic. There is no contamination, symmetry, intrusive-thought-with-neutralization, or magical-undoing pattern.

### 2.7 Dissociative Disorders — EXCLUDED

Despite serial severe trauma, no dissociative phenomena are documented. Identity remains continuous; memory remains intact across stressors; no fugue states; no DID alters (the clones are *literal* externalized fragments, not dissociative alters, and his relationship to them is reflective rather than amnestic). This is itself a noteworthy clinical finding: the secure attachment base appears to have protected against dissociative defense formation, leaving him to metabolize trauma through *cognitive* mechanisms (guilt, rumination) rather than dissociative ones.

### 2.8 Substance Use Disorders — EXCLUDED

No use documented across the canon. As noted above, the operational dangers of disinhibition for an emotion-coupled discharger preclude even normative experimentation.

### 2.9 Attention/Neurodevelopmental — EXCLUDED

Academic achievement is high; sustained attention is intact; executive function is age-appropriate to advanced. No evidence of ADHD, ASD-spectrum features, or specific learning differences.

### 2.10 Psychotic Spectrum — EXCLUDED

No positive symptoms ever documented. Negative symptoms (withdrawal, flat affect) appear only in bereavement context and remit. Reality testing is preserved even during the Civil War II prophecy arc — note that he treats Ulysses's vision as *evidence requiring evaluation*, which is the response of someone with intact reality testing engaging with a genuinely-presented external claim, not delusional ideation.

### 2.11 He Is Not His Uncle

This requires explicit statement because the canon (and Aaron's deathbed pronouncement) plant the suggestion. **Aaron Davis presents with antisocial personality structure**: instrumental relationships including with his nephew; deceitfulness; absence of remorse; criminal lifestyle as identity, not circumstance; willingness to weaponize family bonds. **Miles presents with the inverse profile on every dimension**. The subject's fear of becoming Aaron is itself the strongest possible evidence that he is not Aaron — antisocial personality structure does not generate that fear, because it does not contain the moral apparatus required to produce it. The clone arc (Ahmed run) externalizes and tests this anxiety: when the subject encounters versions of himself displaying Aaron-coded behavior, he refuses to disown or destroy them, instead choosing reparative responsibility. This is not antisocial behavior; it is, structurally, its opposite.

---

## 3. COMORBIDITY ANALYSIS

The features that *are* present cluster in a coherent and mutually reinforcing pattern:

**Survivor guilt** → fuels **impostor phenomenon** (I'm here because they died) → fuels **secret-keeping** (disclosure would impose my chosen burden on others) → fuels **chronic anxiety** (sustained vigilance about consequences) → which **somatically couples** into his powers and creates **environmental feedback** (powers fire on anxiety, producing more events to feel guilty about) → reinforcing survivor guilt.

This is a closed loop with no clinical entry point that requires medication. It is, however, a textbook indication for **trauma-informed adolescent psychotherapy** with attention to *meaning-reconstruction* around inheritance and legitimacy. The subject has never been depicted accessing such care. The informal substitutes — Ganke (peer), Peter (mentor), eventual disclosure to Jefferson (parent) — have been partially effective and account for the slow positive trajectory.

---

## 4. LONGITUDINAL COURSE

**Phase 1 — Acute onset (USM #1–4, ages ~13).** Power onset is experienced as terror. Initial response: refusal. Sub-clinical acute anxiety; no diagnosis warranted.

**Phase 2 — Reluctant adoption (Ultimate Fallout #4 onward).** Onset of survivor guilt as organizing motif. Sub-clinical anxiety, sub-clinical depressive features.

**Phase 3 — Aaron arc and aftermath (USM #22–28+).** First major loss with direct presence. Acute stress features for weeks; resolves to chronic survivor guilt and secret-keeping intensification. Twelve-month withdrawal from costumed activity following.

**Phase 4 — Rio loss (USM #200, Cataclysm).** Most severe symptomatic period. Meets criteria for an Acute Stress Reaction; approaches but does not cross PTSD threshold over subsequent months. Prolonged Grief features present.

**Phase 5 — Secret Wars transition and 616 integration (2015).** Ontological rescue of Rio. Symptoms substantially attenuate; *residue* of hypervigilant attachment and waiting-for-other-shoe cognition persists, without manual analog.

**Phase 6 — Civil War II (2016).** Anticipatory crisis triggered by Ulysses vision. No fresh trauma but reactivation of survivor-guilt/impostor cluster. Self-presents to Captain America for judgment — behaviorally adaptive (help-seeking) even as it indexes the underlying pathology.

**Phase 7 — Champions and stabilization (2016–2019).** Sustained mid-range functioning. Symptoms managed via vocation: the de-escalator/conscience role provides ongoing reparative outlet for survivor guilt.

**Phase 8 — Clone arc / Ahmed run (2018–2022).** Externalized confrontation with shadow-self anxieties. Therapeutically productive within the narrative: he integrates the fear of "bad Miles" by taking responsibility for the clones rather than disowning them. Reduction in (but not resolution of) impostor cluster.

**Phase 9 — Ziglar run / current.** Continued slow trajectory toward self-permission. Subject remains pre-resolution on the central task. No symptom escalation; gradual maturation of self-concept.

**Trajectory summary:** stable to slowly improving over twelve canonical years. No symptom course suggests progression toward formal disorder. Risk factors for future decompensation are bounded and identifiable (see §6).

---

## 5. EXTENDED DIFFERENTIAL — CLOSE CALLS

**Adjustment Disorder with Mixed Anxiety and Depressed Mood:** Considered for the post-Rio period. Rejected because (a) the stressors exceed the "ordinary" character implied by Adjustment Disorder, and (b) his symptom complex carries forward beyond the typical Adjustment Disorder time-course, even as it remains subthreshold for PTSD or MDD. The label *under-describes* what happened.

**Complex PTSD (ICD-11 6B41):** Considered carefully. C-PTSD requires the PTSD core plus disturbances in self-organization (affective dysregulation, negative self-concept, interpersonal disturbances) following sustained or repeated trauma from which escape was difficult or impossible. He has the negative self-concept piece in robust form. He does not have the affective dysregulation piece (he is *over*-regulated). He does not have the interpersonal disturbance piece (he sustains warm, stable relationships). And he never met PTSD criteria proper, which C-PTSD requires as its core. Excluded, but the negative self-concept dimension is the closest single point of contact between his presentation and a formal trauma diagnosis.

**Social Anxiety Disorder:** Considered because of his deference and permission-seeking patterns. Excluded: his deference is *content-specific* (to perceived moral and operational authorities) rather than generalized social-evaluation anxiety. He functions easily in normal social situations; his discomfort is reserved for positions of authority.

**


## Behavioral Atlas

# BEHAVIORAL ATLAS — SUBJECT: MORALES, MILES G.

*Catalog of observed and inferred behavioral signatures across all documented states. Entries are organized by condition, then by channel (postural / kinetic / verbal / paralinguistic / power-coupled / decisional / social). Citations to canon where on-page; inferences from canon-consistent pattern noted as such.*

---

## 1. BASELINE / CALM

The subject's neutral state is the most diagnostic period of any field observation, because every later deviation is read against it.

**Postural signature.** Standing rest: weight slightly forward on the balls of the feet, knees micro-flexed — a sprinter's pre-load that he carries unconsciously since the bite. He does not lock his knees. Seated rest: tendency to perch rather than settle — half on the chair, one foot tucked under, the other planted; on bedroom floor or couch he prefers a corner (back to two walls) over an open seat, even in his own home. In his bedroom (Ganke present) he gravitates to the bed's edge or the floor with his back against the bed frame, rarely the desk chair. Shoulders sit slightly forward and inward; the head tilts a few degrees to his right when listening.

**Hand behavior.** Hands almost never still. Default fidgets include: spinning a pencil through the fingers (school setting, sustained); peeling labels off bottles; picking at the rubberized sole of his sneakers; thumb-rubbing the knuckle of his opposite index finger. Phone-checking is *infrequent* for an adolescent of his cohort — he goes long stretches without looking — but when he does check, it is for parental messages first.

**Gait.** Quick, light, with a habitual *just-not-quite-tracking* tendency to brush walls with his right shoulder/fingertips in narrow corridors — an unconscious wall-adhesion proprioception cue. Walks a touch faster than companions and then slows to recover; never strides. In open public space (a subway platform, the school courtyard) he reads exits within the first three to five seconds of arrival without breaking conversation — a learned habit, not native.

**Voice (calm).** Brooklyn cadence with code-switching that varies by audience: looser, more elision, more AAVE/Nuyorican code with Ganke, with cousins, and on patrol monologue; tighter, more standard, slightly higher pitch with teachers, with Avengers-adjacent adults, and on first meetings. Tends toward an upward inflection at sentence end when uncertain — which, in calm, is most of the time. Laughs easily, often at his own observations a beat before they land.

**Eye behavior.** With family: direct, sustained, soft. With peers: direct, frequently breaking to look at his hands when thinking. With adult authority figures (Rogers, Stark-analog, Drew, T'Challa): a particular pattern — direct on greeting, then slightly downcast during their speech, then back up on his own response. Reads as respectful; functions as deferential.

**Eating.** Large, fast, frequent — metabolic load of the powers. Habitually finishes others' plates with permission. Strong preference for his mother's cooking; will name specific dishes (pernil, arroz con gandules, mofongo when she has time). Eats standing in the kitchen as often as at the table. Drinks water in long pulls, not sips.

**Sleep (calm baseline).** Late to bed, late to rise when permitted. Reads or sketches in bed before sleeping. Sleeps on his side, facing the door — inferred from his alert orientation on wake-ups across the canon.

**Decisional habits (calm).** Defers to the room. In a group choosing where to eat, where to sit, what to do, he will *generate* options but route the choice through Ganke or whoever is most senior. When asked his own preference directly, answers honestly and quickly — the deference is to process, not to repression.

---

## 2. MILD STRESS (school pressure, social friction, minor hero workload)

**Tells, in approximate sequence of appearance.**

1. **Verbal acceleration.** Sentences get faster; filler increases ("like," "I mean," "no, no, wait, I mean"). Self-interruption becomes the dominant grammar.
2. **Humor up-shift.** Jokes increase in frequency and decrease in quality. Self-directed ("I'm an idiot," "this is fine, I'm a functional human"). Notably, in interior monologue (caption boxes across the Bendis and Ahmed runs), the humor is *more* self-critical and *less* funny than what he says aloud — a reliable index of how stressed he actually is versus how stressed he is performing.
3. **Hand-to-face contact.** Palm rubbed across the back of the neck (most frequent); thumb pressed to the brow ridge above the right eye; fingers laced behind the head when seated, elbows out — a posture of accepting the weight of something.
4. **Increased apologizing.** "Sorry" used as a comma. Apologizes for things adjacent to him, not caused by him.
5. **Phone-avoidance.** Stops checking the phone he was barely checking anyway. If a parent texts during a mild-stress window, response is delayed and over-edited.

**Postural shifts.** Shoulders rise toward the ears by perhaps half an inch. The forward-perched seated posture becomes a forward-leaned-elbows-on-knees posture — closed, smaller.

**Power coupling at mild stress.** Nothing fires. Subject has fully trained out involuntary activation at this load. Knuckles may produce a faint static if he is gripping something metal, but this is consciously suppressed and rarely visible to observers.

---

## 3. MODERATE STRESS (sustained workload, secret-keeping pressure, contested decisions, looming threat)

This is the operational state he spends the largest fraction of his life in, and the one with the richest signature.

**Sleep degradation.** First indicator. Lights stay on later; sketching or note-taking in bed; Ganke notices and comments (canonically). On a several-day moderate stress arc, he will fall asleep in clothes, including occasionally in the suit under street clothes. Wakes earlier than his calm baseline, presents at breakfast already pre-fatigued.

**Appetite shift.** Bidirectional. Either eats noticeably less at family meals (which Rio notices immediately) or eats compulsively and joylessly — clearing a plate without looking at it. The mother is the more sensitive instrument; she is the one who calls it.

**Compartmentalization tightens.** This is the most behaviorally visible feature. He becomes a *better liar* under moderate stress, not a worse one — the secret-keeping system goes from background process to foreground discipline. Eye contact with his father during evasive answers becomes *more* steady, not less. Hands disappear into pockets or under the table during these conversations. (The tell that he is lying to Jefferson is therefore not the lie itself but the *symmetry* of his attention — the relaxed asymmetric calm-state listening tilt is replaced by a squared, evenly facing posture. He looks more attentive than he ever otherwise looks at his father.)

**Verbal pattern.** "I'm fine" deployed proactively, in answer to questions not asked. Speech to Ganke becomes elliptical — half-finished sentences trailing off into "...yeah." With Peter, the deference deepens: more "what do you think," fewer self-originated proposals. With Kamala, he is more honest than with any other peer; she gets the closest thing to live affect.

**Movement.** Patrol increases in duration and decreases in purpose. He swings longer, intervenes on smaller incidents, takes more circuitous routes home. The web-line work is technically *better* under moderate stress — more confident, more improvised, more aerial flourish — because the body is happy to be doing something while the mind is not.

**Route patterns under moderate stress.** Strong tendency to return to specific sites: the rooftop two buildings east of Visions Academy that he favored in his first year; the water tower on the block of the Davis apartment that gives sightline on his father coming home; the Brooklyn Bridge cables (north pylon) where he sits with feet dangling when thinking through a problem; the elevated train trestle near Aaron's old apartment, which he does *not* enter but circles. The Aaron site is the diagnostic one — its inclusion in his rotation under moderate stress indicates the load is family-shaped, not school-shaped.

**Power coupling.** Trace involuntary signs return. Fluorescent lights flicker faintly when he passes if he is suppressing a strong feeling (inferred from the bioelectric coupling; canon-adjacent). Camouflage will engage for a fraction of a second under sudden surprise even when no threat is present — a startle ghost. He notices and reasserts visibility within a beat. The blast does not fire at this level.

---

## 4. ACUTE STRESS / THREAT (combat, imminent harm to self or others, identity exposure risk)

**Pre-engagement.** A characteristic three-part sequence in the seconds before contact:
1. A held breath, drawn through the nose, lasting one to two seconds longer than functional.
2. A slight bend at the knees and a roll of the shoulders — the same micro-loading visible in his calm posture, dialed up.
3. A verbal cue, almost always to himself: "okay" or "alright" or "here we go." Audible to mask audio if a mask is on; unconscious.

**Combat signature.** Distinctive and stable across the canon.

- *Movement vocabulary.* Heavy reliance on vertical axis — he goes *up* before going forward, almost reflexively. Engages from above or from a wall, rarely from the ground plane. Webs used as much for redirection (yanking opponents off balance) as for restraint. Combat is *interruptive* rather than terminal — he hits to stop the next action, not to end the fight.
- *Strike economy.* Pulled punches against humans. Visible micro-corrections at point of impact — wrist slack, follow-through arrested. Against non-human or armored opponents the pull is absent and the strikes are noticeably harder, which observers occasionally mistake for cruelty; it is the absence of his habitual restraint, not added force.
- *Venom blast usage.* Conservative. Reserved for: rescue extraction (stunning a single threat to extract a civilian), de-escalation (taking a heavily armed opponent off-line cleanly), and self-defense at close range. He does *not* use it as opening fire. When deployed, accompanied by a vocalized exhalation — a "hah" or grunt, not a quip. The blast is the only one of his abilities he treats with public seriousness.
- *Camouflage usage.* Tactical, deliberate, brief. Used for repositioning and surveillance. He does not fight invisible — partly principle (telegraphs respect for the opponent's situational awareness), partly fatigue (sustained camouflage is taxing, inferred from canon discomfort cues).
- *Quips.* Present but sparser than Parker's. His humor in combat is more frequently directed *at the situation* than at the opponent — observational rather than insulting. Falls silent entirely when civilians are at risk; talkative when alone with the threat. The silence is the alarm bell.

**Verbal pattern under threat.** Three distinct registers:
- *To opponent:* clipped, instructive ("stay down," "don't"). Rarely insults.
- *To civilian:* warm, named if a name is available, instructions short and concrete ("behind me," "run east, two blocks, don't look back").
- *To self:* almost continuous low muttering through the mask — running tactical patter, "okay okay okay," counting beats, naming his next move. This is a regulation tool. He talks himself through.

**Decisional habits under threat.** Civilian-first to a degree that exceeds tactical optimum. Will compromise his own position to interpose. Will accept significant injury to prevent any. Will *not* take a shot that has a non-trivial chance of catastrophic collateral consequence even if the cost of not taking it is high to himself. The decision tree is: civilian safety → containment → opponent welfare → own welfare → mission objective. The reversal of own welfare and opponent welfare is unusual and is the cleanest single behavioral signature of his ethic.

**Power coupling at full acute stress (rare).** Involuntary discharges become possible again — the suppression breaks. When startled at close range or genuinely terrified (not threatened — terrified), the blast fires whether he wills it or not. Camouflage will engage on a fear-spike and hold for several seconds beyond his choosing. This is the single most dangerous and shame-producing failure mode for him; he reads it as a regression to the thirteen-year-old who could not control his body.

---

## 5. INTIMACY (family, romantic, deep friendship)
